      <div id="article-contents" class="article-grid-body"> 
       <h3 id="custom-media-types-for-issues"><a href="#custom-media-types-for-issues">Custom media types for issues</a></h3> 
       <p>These are the supported media types for issues.</p> 
       <pre><code>application/vnd.github.VERSION.raw+json
application/vnd.github.VERSION.text+json
application/vnd.github.VERSION.html+json
application/vnd.github.VERSION.full+json
</code></pre> 
       <p>For more information about media types, see "<a href="/en/rest/overview/media-types">Custom media types</a>."</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user">List issues assigned to the authenticated user</a> </h3> 
         <p>List issues assigned to the authenticated user across all visible repositories including owned repositories, member repositories, and organization repositories. You can use the <code>filter</code> query parameter to fetch issues that are not necessarily assigned to you.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: GitHub's REST API v3 considers every pull request an issue, but not every issue is a pull request. For this reason, "Issues" endpoints may return both issues and pull requests in the response. You can identify pull requests by the <code>pull_request</code> key. Be aware that the <code>id</code> of a pull request returned from "Issues" endpoints will be an <em>issue id</em>. To find out the pull request id, use the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/pulls#list-pull-requests">List pull requests</a>" endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /issues</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--parameters"> <a href="#list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>filter</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates which sorts of issues to return. Can be one of:<br> * <code>assigned</code>: Issues assigned to you<br> * <code>created</code>: Issues created by you<br> * <code>mentioned</code>: Issues mentioning you<br> * <code>subscribed</code>: Issues you're subscribed to updates for<br> * <code>all</code>: All issues the authenticated user can see, regardless of participation or creation</p> Default: <code>assigned</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>state</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates the state of the issues to return. Can be either <code>open</code>, <code>closed</code>, or <code>all</code>.</p> Default: <code>open</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A list of comma separated label names. Example: <code>bug,ui,@high</code></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>What to sort results by. Can be either <code>created</code>, <code>updated</code>, <code>comments</code>.</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Only show notifications updated after the given time. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>collab</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>orgs</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owned</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>pulls</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">boolean</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--code-samples"> <a href="#list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/issues</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /issues'</span>)
</code></pre>

         <h4>Validation failed</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 422 Unprocessable Entity</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4 id="list-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user">List organization issues assigned to the authenticated user</a> </h3> 
         <p>List issues in an organization assigned to the authenticated user.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: GitHub's REST API v3 considers every pull request an issue, but not every issue is a pull request. For this reason, "Issues" endpoints may return both issues and pull requests in the response. You can identify pull requests by the <code>pull_request</code> key. Be aware that the <code>id</code> of a pull request returned from "Issues" endpoints will be an <em>issue id</em>. To find out the pull request id, use the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/pulls#list-pull-requests">List pull requests</a>" endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /orgs/{org}/issues</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--parameters"> <a href="#list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>org</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>filter</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates which sorts of issues to return. Can be one of:<br> * <code>assigned</code>: Issues assigned to you<br> * <code>created</code>: Issues created by you<br> * <code>mentioned</code>: Issues mentioning you<br> * <code>subscribed</code>: Issues you're subscribed to updates for<br> * <code>all</code>: All issues the authenticated user can see, regardless of participation or creation</p> Default: <code>assigned</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>state</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates the state of the issues to return. Can be either <code>open</code>, <code>closed</code>, or <code>all</code>.</p> Default: <code>open</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A list of comma separated label names. Example: <code>bug,ui,@high</code></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>What to sort results by. Can be either <code>created</code>, <code>updated</code>, <code>comments</code>.</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Only show notifications updated after the given time. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--code-samples"> <a href="#list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/orgs/ORG/issues</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /orgs/{org}/issues'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">org</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'org'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4 id="list-organization-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-repository-issues" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-repository-issues">List repository issues</a> </h3> 
         <p>List issues in a repository.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: GitHub's REST API v3 considers every pull request an issue, but not every issue is a pull request. For this reason, "Issues" endpoints may return both issues and pull requests in the response. You can identify pull requests by the <code>pull_request</code> key. Be aware that the <code>id</code> of a pull request returned from "Issues" endpoints will be an <em>issue id</em>. To find out the pull request id, use the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/pulls#list-pull-requests">List pull requests</a>" endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-repository-issues--parameters"> <a href="#list-repository-issues--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-repository-issues-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>milestone</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>If an <code>integer</code> is passed, it should refer to a milestone by its <code>number</code> field. If the string <code>*</code> is passed, issues with any milestone are accepted. If the string <code>none</code> is passed, issues without milestones are returned.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>state</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates the state of the issues to return. Can be either <code>open</code>, <code>closed</code>, or <code>all</code>.</p> Default: <code>open</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignee</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Can be the name of a user. Pass in <code>none</code> for issues with no assigned user, and <code>*</code> for issues assigned to any user.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>creator</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The user that created the issue.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>mentioned</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A user that's mentioned in the issue.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A list of comma separated label names. Example: <code>bug,ui,@high</code></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>What to sort results by. Can be either <code>created</code>, <code>updated</code>, <code>comments</code>.</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Only show notifications updated after the given time. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-repository-issues--code-samples"> <a href="#list-repository-issues--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="list-repository-issues-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-an-issue">Create an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Any user with pull access to a repository can create an issue. If <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/disabling-issues/">issues are disabled in the repository</a>, the API returns a <code>410 Gone</code> status.</p> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-abuse-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#create-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The title of the issue.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The contents of the issue.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignee</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Login for the user that this issue should be assigned to. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set the assignee for new issues. The assignee is silently dropped otherwise. <strong>This field is deprecated.</strong></em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>milestone</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or integer or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The <code>number</code> of the milestone to associate this issue with. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set the milestone for new issues. The milestone is silently dropped otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings or array of objects</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Labels to associate with this issue. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set labels for new issues. Labels are silently dropped otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignees</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Logins for Users to assign to this issue. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set assignees for new issues. Assignees are silently dropped otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="create-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#create-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues \
  -d '{"title":"title"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'title'</span>
})
</code></pre>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-issue">Get an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>The API returns a <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-redirects-redirects"><code>301 Moved Permanently</code> status</a> if the issue was <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/transferring-an-issue-to-another-repository/">transferred</a> to another repository. If the issue was transferred to or deleted from a repository where the authenticated user lacks read access, the API returns a <code>404 Not Found</code> status. If the issue was deleted from a repository where the authenticated user has read access, the API returns a <code>410 Gone</code> status. To receive webhook events for transferred and deleted issues, subscribe to the <a href="https://docs.github.com/webhooks/event-payloads/#issues"><code>issues</code></a> webhook.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: GitHub's REST API v3 considers every pull request an issue, but not every issue is a pull request. For this reason, "Issues" endpoints may return both issues and pull requests in the response. You can identify pull requests by the <code>pull_request</code> key. Be aware that the <code>id</code> of a pull request returned from "Issues" endpoints will be an <em>issue id</em>. To find out the pull request id, use the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/pulls#list-pull-requests">List pull requests</a>" endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#get-an-issue-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#get-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">issue_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Moved permanently</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 301 Moved Permanently</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Not modified</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 304 Not Modified</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Resource not found</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Gone</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 410 Gone</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="update-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#update-an-issue">Update an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Issue owners and users with push access can edit an issue.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">patch</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="update-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#update-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or integer or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The title of the issue.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The contents of the issue.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignee</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Login for the user that this issue should be assigned to. <strong>This field is deprecated.</strong></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>state</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>State of the issue. Either <code>open</code> or <code>closed</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>milestone</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string or integer or nullable</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The <code>number</code> of the milestone to associate this issue with or <code>null</code> to remove current. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set the milestone for issues. The milestone is silently dropped otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings or array of objects</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Labels to associate with this issue. Pass one or more Labels to <em>replace</em> the set of Labels on this Issue. Send an empty array (<code>[]</code>) to clear all Labels from the Issue. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set labels for issues. Labels are silently dropped otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignees</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Logins for Users to assign to this issue. Pass one or more user logins to <em>replace</em> the set of assignees on this Issue. Send an empty array (<code>[]</code>) to clear all assignees from the Issue. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can set assignees for new issues. Assignees are silently dropped otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="update-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#update-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PATCH \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/42 \
  -d '{"title":"title"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PATCH /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">issue_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">title</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'title'</span>
})
</code></pre>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="lock-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#lock-an-issue">Lock an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Users with push access can lock an issue or pull request's conversation.</p> 
         <p>Note that, if you choose not to pass any parameters, you'll need to set <code>Content-Length</code> to zero when calling out to this endpoint. For more information, see "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#http-verbs">HTTP verbs</a>."</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/lock</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="lock-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#lock-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>lock_reason</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The reason for locking the issue or pull request conversation. Lock will fail if you don't use one of these reasons:<br> * <code>off-topic</code><br> * <code>too heated</code><br> * <code>resolved</code><br> * <code>spam</code></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="lock-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#lock-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X PUT \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/42/lock \
  -d '{"lock_reason":"lock_reason"}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'PUT /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/lock'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">issue_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">lock_reason</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'lock_reason'</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>Response</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Forbidden</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 403 Forbidden</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Resource not found</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Gone</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 410 Gone</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Validation failed</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 422 Unprocessable Entity</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user">List user account issues assigned to the authenticated user</a> </h3> 
         <p>List issues across owned and member repositories assigned to the authenticated user.</p> 
         <p><strong>Note</strong>: GitHub's REST API v3 considers every pull request an issue, but not every issue is a pull request. For this reason, "Issues" endpoints may return both issues and pull requests in the response. You can identify pull requests by the <code>pull_request</code> key. Be aware that the <code>id</code> of a pull request returned from "Issues" endpoints will be an <em>issue id</em>. To find out the pull request id, use the "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/pulls#list-pull-requests">List pull requests</a>" endpoint.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /user/issues</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--parameters"> <a href="#list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>filter</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates which sorts of issues to return. Can be one of:<br> * <code>assigned</code>: Issues assigned to you<br> * <code>created</code>: Issues created by you<br> * <code>mentioned</code>: Issues mentioning you<br> * <code>subscribed</code>: Issues you're subscribed to updates for<br> * <code>all</code>: All issues the authenticated user can see, regardless of participation or creation</p> Default: <code>assigned</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>state</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Indicates the state of the issues to return. Can be either <code>open</code>, <code>closed</code>, or <code>all</code>.</p> Default: <code>open</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A list of comma separated label names. Example: <code>bug,ui,@high</code></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>What to sort results by. Can be either <code>created</code>, <code>updated</code>, <code>comments</code>.</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>asc</code> (ascending) or <code>desc</code> (descending).</p> Default: <code>desc</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Only show notifications updated after the given time. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--code-samples"> <a href="#list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5>

  https://api.github.com/user/issues</code></pre>

    <span class="hljs-attr">"author_association"</span>: <span class="hljs-string">"COLLABORATOR"</span>
  }
]
</code></pre>
         </div> 
         <h4>Not modified</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 304 Not Modified</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Resource not found</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4 id="list-user-account-issues-assigned-to-the-authenticated-user-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <h2 id="assignees"><a href="#assignees">Assignees</a></h2> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-assignees" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-assignees">List assignees</a> </h3> 
         <p>Lists the <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/assigning-issues-and-pull-requests-to-other-github-users/">available assignees</a> for issues in a repository.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/assignees</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-assignees--parameters"> <a href="#list-assignees--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="check-if-a-user-can-be-assigned" class="pt-3"> <a href="#check-if-a-user-can-be-assigned">Check if a user can be assigned</a> </h3> 
         <p>Checks if a user has permission to be assigned to an issue in this repository.</p> 
         <p>If the <code>assignee</code> can be assigned to issues in the repository, a <code>204</code> header with no content is returned.</p> 
         <p>Otherwise a <code>404</code> status code is returned.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/assignees/{assignee}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="check-if-a-user-can-be-assigned--parameters"> <a href="#check-if-a-user-can-be-assigned--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignee</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="check-if-a-user-can-be-assigned--code-samples"> <a href="#check-if-a-user-can-be-assigned--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/assignees/ASSIGNEE</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/assignees/{assignee}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">assignee</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'assignee'</span>
})
</code></pre> 
         <h4>If the `assignee` can be assigned to issues in the repository, a `204` header with no content is returned.</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 204 No Content</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Otherwise a `404` status code is returned.</h4> 
         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2">

        <div> 
         <h3 id="add-assignees-to-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-assignees-to-an-issue">Add assignees to an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Adds up to 10 assignees to an issue. Users already assigned to an issue are not replaced.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/assignees</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-assignees-to-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#add-assignees-to-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignees</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Usernames of people to assign this issue to. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can add assignees to an issue. Assignees are silently ignored otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="add-assignees-to-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#add-assignees-to-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/42/assignees \
  -d '{"assignees":["assignees"]}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/assignees'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">issue_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">assignees</span>: [
    <span class="hljs-string">'assignees'</span>
  ]
})
</code></pre>

       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="remove-assignees-from-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-assignees-from-an-issue">Remove assignees from an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Removes one or more assignees from an issue.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">delete</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/assignees</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="remove-assignees-from-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#remove-assignees-from-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>assignees</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Usernames of assignees to remove from an issue. <em>NOTE: Only users with push access can remove assignees from an issue. Assignees are silently ignored otherwise.</em></p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="remove-assignees-from-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#remove-assignees-from-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X DELETE \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/42/assignees \
  -d '{"assignees":["assignees"]}'</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'DELETE /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/assignees'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">issue_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">assignees</span>: [
    <span class="hljs-string">'assignees'</span>
  ]
})
</code></pre>

       <h2 id="comments"><a href="#comments">Comments</a></h2> 
       <p>The Issue Comments API supports listing, viewing, editing, and creating comments on issues and pull requests.</p> 
       <p>Issue Comments use <a href="#custom-media-types">these custom media types</a>. You can read more about the use of media types in the API <a href="/en/rest/overview/media-types">here</a>.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-issue-comments-for-a-repository" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-issue-comments-for-a-repository">List issue comments for a repository</a> </h3> 
         <p>By default, Issue Comments are ordered by ascending ID.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/comments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-issue-comments-for-a-repository--parameters"> <a href="#list-issue-comments-for-a-repository--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-issue-comments-for-a-repository-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>sort</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>One of <code>created</code> (when the repository was starred) or <code>updated</code> (when it was last pushed to).</p> Default: <code>created</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>direction</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Either <code>asc</code> or <code>desc</code>. Ignored without the <code>sort</code> parameter.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>since</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Only show notifications updated after the given time. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-issue-comments-for-a-repository--code-samples"> <a href="#list-issue-comments-for-a-repository--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/comments</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/comments'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div>

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="list-issue-comments-for-a-repository-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-issue-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-issue-comment">Get an issue comment</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/comments/{comment_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue-comment--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-issue-comment--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#get-an-issue-comment-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>comment_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>comment_id parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <pre><code>Status: 404 Not Found</code></pre> 
         <div class="height-constrained-code-block"></div> 
         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue-comment-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>An additional <code>reactions</code> object in the issue comment payload is currently available for developers to preview. During the preview period, the APIs may change without advance notice. Please see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2016-05-12-reactions-api-preview">blog post</a> for full details.</p> 
          <p>To access the API you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.squirrel-girl-preview</code></pre> 
          <p>The <code>reactions</code> key will have the following payload where <code>url</code> can be used to construct the API location for <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/reference/reactions">listing and creating</a> reactions.</p> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div>

        <div> 
         <h3 id="create-an-issue-comment" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-an-issue-comment">Create an issue comment</a> </h3> 
         <p>This endpoint triggers <a href="https://docs.github.com/en/github/managing-subscriptions-and-notifications-on-github/about-notifications">notifications</a>. Creating content too quickly using this endpoint may result in abuse rate limiting. See "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/resources-in-the-rest-api#abuse-rate-limits">Abuse rate limits</a>" and "<a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/guides/best-practices-for-integrators#dealing-with-abuse-rate-limits">Dealing with abuse rate limits</a>" for details.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/comments</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-an-issue-comment--parameters"> <a href="#create-an-issue-comment--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>body</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The contents of the comment.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -X POST \

         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'POST /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/comments'</span>, {
