       <h2 id="events"><a href="#events">Events</a></h2> 
       <p>The Issue Events API can return different types of events triggered by activity in issues and pull requests. For more information about the specific events that you can receive from the Issue Events API, see "<a href="/en/developers/webhooks-and-events/issue-event-types">Issue event types</a>." An events API for GitHub activity outside of issues and pull requests is also available. For more information, see the "<a href="/en/developers/webhooks-and-events/github-event-types">Events API</a>."</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-issue-events-for-a-repository" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-issue-events-for-a-repository">List issue events for a repository</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/events</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-issue-events-for-a-repository--parameters"> <a href="#list-issue-events-for-a-repository--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#list-issue-events-for-a-repository-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-issue-events-for-a-repository--code-samples"> <a href="#list-issue-events-for-a-repository--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/events</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/events'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4>Notes</h4> 
         <ul class="mt-2"> 
          <li><a href="/en/developers/apps">Works with GitHub Apps</a></li> 
         </ul> 
         <h4 id="list-issue-events-for-a-repository-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>Project card details are now shown in REST API v3 responses for project-related issue and timeline events. This feature is now available for developers to preview. For details, see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2018-09-05-project-card-events">blog post</a>.</p> 
          <p>To receive the <code>project_card</code> attribute, project boards must be <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/disabling-project-boards-in-a-repository">enabled</a> for a repository, and you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.starfox-preview+json</code></pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="get-an-issue-event" class="pt-3"> <a href="#get-an-issue-event">Get an issue event</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/events/{event_id}</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue-event--parameters"> <a href="#get-an-issue-event--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. <a href="#get-an-issue-event-preview-notices"> See preview notice </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>event_id</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="get-an-issue-event--code-samples"> <a href="#get-an-issue-event--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/events/42</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/events/{event_id}'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">event_id</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>
})
</code></pre>

         <h4 id="get-an-issue-event-preview-notices"> Preview notice </h4> 
         <div class="extended-markdown note border rounded-1 mb-4 p-3 color-border-info color-bg-info f5"> 
          <p>Project card details are now shown in REST API v3 responses for project-related issue and timeline events. This feature is now available for developers to preview. For details, see the <a href="https://developer.github.com/changes/2018-09-05-project-card-events">blog post</a>.</p> 
          <p>To receive the <code>project_card</code> attribute, project boards must be <a href="https://help.github.com/articles/disabling-project-boards-in-a-repository">enabled</a> for a repository, and you must provide a custom <a href="https://docs.github.com/rest/overview/media-types">media type</a> in the <code>Accept</code> header:</p> 
          <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">application/vnd.github.starfox-preview+json</code></pre> 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <hr> 
       </div>

         <h3 id="add-labels-to-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#add-labels-to-an-issue">Add labels to an issue</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/labels</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="add-labels-to-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#add-labels-to-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>labels</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">array of strings</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The names of the labels to add to the issue. You can pass an empty array to remove all labels. <strong>Note:</strong> Alternatively, you can pass a single label as a <code>string</code> or an <code>array</code> of labels directly, but GitHub recommends passing an object with the <code>labels</code> key.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

         <h3 id="set-labels-for-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#set-labels-for-an-issue">Set labels for an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Removes any previous labels and sets the new labels for an issue.</p> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">put</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/labels</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="set-labels-for-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#set-labels-for-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          -->

         <h3 id="remove-a-label-from-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#remove-a-label-from-an-issue">Remove a label from an issue</a> </h3> 
         <p>Removes the specified label from the issue, and returns the remaining labels on the issue. This endpoint returns a <code>404 Not Found</code> status if the label does not exist.</p>

         <h3 id="create-a-label" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-label">Create a label</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/labels</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-label--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-label--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>name</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The name of the label. Emoji can be added to label names, using either native emoji or colon-style markup. For example, typing <code>:strawberry:</code> will render the emoji <img src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f353.png" alt=":strawberry:" title=":strawberry:">. For a full list of available emoji and codes, see "<a href="https://github.com/ikatyang/emoji-cheat-sheet">Emoji cheat sheet</a>."</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>color</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The <a href="http://www.color-hex.com/">hexadecimal color code</a> for the label, without the leading <code>#</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>description</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A short description of the label.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The new name of the label. Emoji can be added to label names, using either native emoji or colon-style markup. For example, typing <code>:strawberry:</code> will render the emoji <img src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f353.png" alt=":strawberry:" title=":strawberry:">.          <h3 id="create-a-milestone" class="pt-3"> <a href="#create-a-milestone">Create a milestone</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">post</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/milestones</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="create-a-milestone--parameters"> <a href="#create-a-milestone--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> Setting to <code>application/vnd.github.v3+json</code> is recommended. </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>title</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p><strong>Required</strong>. The title of the milestone.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>state</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The state of the milestone. Either <code>open</code> or <code>closed</code>.</p> Default: <code>open</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>description</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>A description of the milestone.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>due_on</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">body</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>The milestone due date. This is a timestamp in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ISO_8601">ISO 8601</a> format: <code>YYYY-MM-DDTHH:MM:SSZ</code>.</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table>

  -X POST \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.v3+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/milestones \
  -d '{"title":"title"}'</code></pre>

       <h2 id="timeline"><a href="#timeline">Timeline</a></h2> 
       <p>The Timeline Events API can return different types of events triggered by timeline activity in issues and pull requests. For more information about the specific events that you can receive from the Issue Events API, see "<a href="/en/developers/webhooks-and-events/issue-event-types">Issue event types</a>." An events API for GitHub activity outside of issues and pull requests is also available. For more information, see the "<a href="/en/developers/webhooks-and-events/github-event-types">GitHub Events API</a>."</p> 
       <p>You can use this API to display information about issues and pull request or determine who should be notified of issue comments.</p> 
       <div> 
        <div> 
         <h3 id="list-timeline-events-for-an-issue" class="pt-3"> <a href="#list-timeline-events-for-an-issue">List timeline events for an issue</a> </h3> 
        </div> 
        <pre><code><span class="color-bg-info-inverse color-text-inverse rounded-1 px-2 py-1" style="text-transform: uppercase">get</span> /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/timeline</code></pre> 
        <div> 
         <h4 id="list-timeline-events-for-an-issue--parameters"> <a href="#list-timeline-events-for-an-issue--parameters">Parameters</a> </h4> 
         <table> 
          <thead> 
           <tr> 
            <th>Name</th> 
            <th>Type</th> 
            <th>In</th> 
            <th>Description</th> 
           </tr> 
          </thead> 
          <tbody> <!--
            Previews require an `accept` header. These used to be documented
            as `operation.parameters` but have moved to `operation.x-github.previews`
          --> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>accept</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">header</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p> This API is under preview and subject to change. <a href="#list-timeline-events-for-an-issue-preview-notices"> See preview notices </a> </p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>owner</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>repo</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">string</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>issue_number</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">path</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>issue_number parameter</p> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>per_page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Results per page (max 100).</p> Default: <code>30</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
           <tr> 
            <td><code>page</code></td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">integer</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70">query</td> 
            <td class="opacity-70"> <p>Page number of the results to fetch.</p> Default: <code>1</code> </td> 
           </tr> 
          </tbody> 
         </table> 
         <h4 id="list-timeline-events-for-an-issue--code-samples"> <a href="#list-timeline-events-for-an-issue--code-samples">Code samples</a> </h4> 
         <h5> Shell </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-shell">curl \
  -H "Accept: application/vnd.github.mockingbird-preview+json" \
  https://api.github.com/repos/octocat/hello-world/issues/42/timeline</code></pre> 
         <h5> JavaScript (<a href="https://github.com/octokit/core.js#readme">@octokit/core.js</a>) </h5> 
         <pre><code class="hljs language-javascript"><span class="hljs-keyword">await</span> octokit.request(<span class="hljs-string">'GET /repos/{owner}/{repo}/issues/{issue_number}/timeline'</span>, {
  <span class="hljs-attr">owner</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'octocat'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">repo</span>: <span class="hljs-string">'hello-world'</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">issue_number</span>: <span class="hljs-number">42</span>,
  <span class="hljs-attr">mediaType</span>: {
    <span class="hljs-attr">previews</span>: [
      <span class="hljs-string">'mockingbird'</span>
    ]
  }
})
</code></pre>
